SELECT EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY AS [loan_number], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LOANAMT AS [loan_amount], LN_CODES_30.CODEDESC AS [loan_status], EMPOWER.LN_PROPINFO.PROP_STATE AS [property_state], B1.BORR_LAST AS [borrower_last], ITP.CAMPAIGN_NAME AS [campaign_name], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.APPRAISEDVAL AS [appraised_value], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.INTRATE AS [interest_rate], EMPOWER.LN_PLANDAT.LPLANDESC AS [loan_plan_name], LN_CODES_4.CODEDESC AS [loan_purpose], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LTV AS [ltv], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.CLTV AS [cltv], EMPOWER.LN_PLANDAT.DISCFEE AS [discfee], (SELECT SUM(BORRPART) FROM EMPOWER.LN_FEES WHERE LN_FEES.LNKEY=EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY AND (HUDNUMBER < 900 OR HUDNUMBER >= 1100)) AS [TOTFEES], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LOCKINEXPIRES AS [lock_expiration], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.EXPCLOSEDATE AS [expected_close_date], EMPOWER.LN_DOCGEN.SETTLEMENT_DATE AS [settlement_date], EMPOWER.LN_CONTACTS.LOAN_OFFICER AS [loan_officer], EMPOWER.LN_CONTACTS.PROCESSOR AS [processor], EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD.DESCRIPTION AS [notepad_item]
FROM EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_CODES AS LN_CODES_30 ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = LN_CODES_30.LNKEY AND LN_CODES_30.IDX=30
INNER JOIN EMPOWER.LN_PROPINFO ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_PROPINFO.LNKEY
INNER JOIN EMPOWER.LN_BORRINFO AS B1 ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = B1.LNKEY AND B1.WHICHBORR=1
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_INTVWPROCESS AS ITP ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = ITP.LNKEY
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_PLANDAT ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_PLANDAT.LNKEY
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_CODES AS LN_CODES_4 ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = LN_CODES_4.LNKEY AND LN_CODES_4.IDX=4
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_DOCGEN ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_DOCGEN.LNKEY
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_CONTACTS ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_CONTACTS.LNKEY
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD.LNKEY AND EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD.IDX=(SELECT MAX(IDX) FROM EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD NP2 WHERE NP2.LNKEY=EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD.LNKEY)
LEFT JOIN LOOKUP ON LOOKUP.STATUS = LN_CODES_30.CODEINT
WHERE LN_CODES_30.CODEDESC IN (@filter_0_0, @filter_0_1, @filter_0_2, @filter_0_3, @filter_0_4, @filter_0_5, @filter_0_6, @filter_0_7, @filter_0_8, @filter_0_9) AND (AND DATEDIFF(DAY,(SELECT TOP 1 DATES FROM EMPOWER.LN_EVENTS EV WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE EV.LNKEY=EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY AND EVENTNUM=LU.EVENTNUM ORDER BY IDX DESC),GETDATE())=0)
ORDER BY EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY ASC

SELECT EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY AS [loan_number], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LOANAMT AS [loan_amount], LN_CODES_30.CODEDESC AS [loan_status], EMPOWER.LN_PROPINFO.PROP_STATE AS [property_state], B1.BORR_LAST AS [borrower_last], ITP.CAMPAIGN_NAME AS [campaign_name], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.APPRAISEDVAL AS [appraised_value], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.INTRATE AS [interest_rate], EMPOWER.LN_PLANDAT.LPLANDESC AS [loan_plan_name], LN_CODES_4.CODEDESC AS [loan_purpose], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LTV AS [ltv], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.CLTV AS [cltv], EMPOWER.LN_PLANDAT.DISCFEE AS [discfee], (SELECT SUM(BORRPART) FROM EMPOWER.LN_FEES WHERE LN_FEES.LNKEY=EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY AND (HUDNUMBER < 900 OR HUDNUMBER >= 1100)) AS [TOTFEES], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LOCKINEXPIRES AS [lock_expiration], EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.EXPCLOSEDATE AS [expected_close_date], EMPOWER.LN_DOCGEN.SETTLEMENT_DATE AS [settlement_date], EMPOWER.LN_CONTACTS.LOAN_OFFICER AS [loan_officer], EMPOWER.LN_CONTACTS.PROCESSOR AS [processor], EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD.DESCRIPTION AS [notepad_item]
FROM EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_CODES AS LN_CODES_30 ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = LN_CODES_30.LNKEY AND LN_CODES_30.IDX=30
INNER JOIN EMPOWER.LN_PROPINFO ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_PROPINFO.LNKEY
INNER JOIN EMPOWER.LN_BORRINFO AS B1 ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = B1.LNKEY AND B1.WHICHBORR=1
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_INTVWPROCESS AS ITP ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = ITP.LNKEY
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_PLANDAT ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_PLANDAT.LNKEY
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_CODES AS LN_CODES_4 ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = LN_CODES_4.LNKEY AND LN_CODES_4.IDX=4
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_DOCGEN ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_DOCGEN.LNKEY
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_CONTACTS ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_CONTACTS.LNKEY
LEFT JOIN EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD ON EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY = EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD.LNKEY AND EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD.IDX=(SELECT MAX(IDX) FROM EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD NP2 WHERE NP2.LNKEY=EMPOWER.LN_NOTEPAD.LNKEY)
LEFT JOIN LOOKUP ON LOOKUP.STATUS = LN_CODES_30.CODEINT
WHERE LN_CODES_30.CODEDESC IN (@filter_0_0, @filter_0_1, @filter_0_2, @filter_0_3, @filter_0_4, @filter_0_5, @filter_0_6, @filter_0_7, @filter_0_8, @filter_0_9) AND (DATEDIFF(DAY,(SELECT TOP 1 DATES FROM EMPOWER.LN_EVENTS EV WITH (NOLOCK) WHERE EV.LNKEY=EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY AND EV.EVENTNUM=LOOKUP.EVENTNUM ORDER BY EV.IDX DESC),GETDATE())=0)
ORDER BY EMPOWER.LN_MTGTERMS.LNKEY ASC
OFFSET @_offset ROWS
FETCH NEXT @_pageSize ROWS ONLY
 with parameters: @filter_0_0=Cleared, @filter_0_1=Code Red, @filter_0_2=Docs In, @filter_0_3=Docs Out, @filter_0_4=Docs Rev, @filter_0_5=In Proc, @filter_0_6=Pending Cancel, @filter_0_7=Pre-Approval, @filter_0_8=Pre-Docs, @filter_0_9=Subordination, @_offset=0, @_pageSize=50000
